### Quora -  Astrological Question and Answers by Steve Hora
{{< rawhtml >}}
<div><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What's the compatibility of a Libra Sun/Leo Moon man and a Leo Sun/Aries Moon woman?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This reading will be as per western astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A Libra Sun man will aspire for a Leo Sun woman or vice-versa, only for each others appreciation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A Leo Moon man is proud and self-sustained in emotions and a Aries Moon woman is energetic and freedom seeking. Both admire each other from a distance and go their own way.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">We have NOT touched upon the psychological, emotional, thinking compatibility. There are other physical, psychological, sexual and spiritual compatibility, which cannot be read with this sparse data of yours.</p><ul><li><b>For thorough Analysis of matching</b></li><li>If both persons <b>Sun sign, Moon Sign and Ascendant are given</b>, it will be generic matching with a 10% accuracy</li><li>If both persons Sun sign, Moon Sign and Ascendant <b>and dispositors are given</b>, it will be a matching with a 50% accuracy.</li><li>With accurate birth details of both, expect 95% accuracy and if a very particular question of relationship, is asked.</li><li>5% deviation - I give it to cesarean births, both Time of birth can be, not accurate, within 5 minutes or wrong or software I use.</li><li>With birth details, one can say what is the present planetary period for you to choose, which kind of person and with what sun, moon and ascendant sign should be, for best compatibility in all of relationship attributes.</li><li>I follow Whole-Sign-house system, transits and metonic-cycle timing analysis for a western astrological reading.</li><li>Personal questions can be asked, if you have private problems or privacy concerns. I will reply to you, ASAP.</li><li>I will answer as soon as possible, based on the number of queries. But I will strive to answer within a week. For a quick reply also, send horoscope details.</li></ul></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 05:28 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the results of Saturn and venus being conjunct in Scorpio in the 12th house?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Saturn - Shani as 2nd and 3rd lord in 12th, and Venus - Shukra as 6th and 11th, both in 12th of Scorpio - Vrischika Lagna, is not good for wealth, co-borns and finance. Only good for health.</p><ul><li><b>For thorough astrological Analysis and vedic horoscope reading of your question</b></li><ul><li>Ask with your <b>birth details.<br /></b>e.g. &#8220;What can be read about marriage and when I will get married, my birth details : 4th Sep 1986, 21:34 PM, Mumbai, India&#8221;.</li><li>You can have a true and accurate reading of a life question which will contain the following</li><ul><li>For each specific life question or problem, astrological analysis, solution and accurate timing of the event to happen</li><li>Solution to the problem with astrological and psychological advice</li><li>Remedies or Dosha or Ill-effect, if needed to be removed</li><li>Color therapy or Gem recommendation</li><li>Specific Graha Mantra and time to do the mantra prayog , for the event to happen</li><li>Other mantras for general protection</li></ul></ul><li><b>if the question is not with birth details, </b>the prediction will be as below.</li><ul><li>Generic Prediction with 10% accuracy and with no timing.</li><li>With nakshatra pada positions of the said grahas is made available, expect another 25% accuracy.</li><li>With navamsa positions of the all grahas is made available, expect 50% accuracy.</li><li>With other divisional charts are there, expect 75% accuracy.</li><li>With Vimshottari dasha details, expect 85% accuracy.</li><li>With full chart and accurate birth details, it becomes reading and will be 95%, from me.</li><li>I use NadiAmsa where time (Vimshottari) and Space (Graha-House owners) meet, which is 95% accurate.</li><li>5% deviation - I give it to cesarean births, your Time of birth can be not accurate within 5 minutes or wrong, ayanamsa not correct, software I use, year duration I use.</li></ul></ul></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 05:33 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Does my astrological horoscope show any indication of success as a litigation lawyer (DOB 13-08-1984, time 16:00, and in Mumbai)?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hi <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/User-13085030390467539287">User-13085030390467539287</a></span>,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Your chart Analysis and Reading as per Vedic Astrology </b>:</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Casting your vedic horoscope according to Lahiri Ayanamsa (Chitra paksha) and using sidereal solar years of 360 and using Vimshottari Dasha and NadiAmsa timing technique.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I am using fixed house lagna chart, not bhava chalit chart which creates delineation problems in amsa charts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Career Success :</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">10th lord Budha is in 9th with 11th. But 9th lord is in 8th. Inherently you are reflecting, that you would be a failure, due to the graha placement.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Also Guru is retrograde, which slows down your growth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Dasamsa shows no promise.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">You would be better of handling litigation regarding heredity property and divorce.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-5eaaa6f787be546aa41796b78ec8bc26" master_src="/img/qimg-5eaaa6f787be546aa41796b78ec8bc26" master_w="793" master_h="1123" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 06:07 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the significance of Saturn in astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani being a karmic Graha, has to uphold karma. Based on your balance sheet of karma, Shani will deliver your goods in this birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The significance varies as per the Dasha and transit</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Refer</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/What-are-the-ill-effects-of-Ashtama-shani-during-the-next-one-and-half-years-for-Aries-sign">What are the ill effects of Ashtama shani during the next one and half years for Aries sign?</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani Sade Sati, the most dreaded transition of the Great Karmic Graha - Shani.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani is a karmic Graha and takes nearly 30 years to make a full cycle of the zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As he passes through the 12th, 1st and 2nd of one&#8217;s Rashi or Moon sign (Vedic), which is about 7.5 years, Sade Sati occurs.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The very karmic nature of Shani is to note down the good and bad karma of a person from previous birth, then.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In this birth bestow the person with good karma and punish for bad karma.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In the present life, he will note down all good and bad karma and carry-over to next birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">IF, the good karma CANCELS the bad one, and exceeds, then Shani will NOT harm in the coming Sade Sati.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the remedy is DOING good karma. Many make money by defining remedy in many ways according to their business - braminical, mantric, tantric, la-ketabic and what not.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shani understands only one remedy, that is your help to the very needy, so be it, the good karma.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 06:15 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is important, Lagna or Rashi? Which is the best to analyze a horoscope?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna is calculated based on the Sun&#8217;s position and the horizon at the time of birth, on earth. Inherently it means and denotes the physical body and from there the material world as lived upon this earth. That is why, the house counting and the significance is based on lagna.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That said Rashi or Moon-sign or moon-nakshatra, precisely, is taken as the reference to delineate, the changes that is going to affect this lagna and its houses, by way of time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From above you find both are important for analysis of the horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It takes some research and understanding to know the inner working of lagna and rashi, not ad-literam quoting from scripts or from experience, which is just one another opinion.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Moon as a graha by itself reflects Sun&#8217;s ray at night and in day also, to create the lunatic affectation on earthlings. Here Chandra also plays a double role as karaka and time-karaka.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 06:54 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How does relocation astrology (astrocartography) work?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrocartography or Relocation astrology was there in vedic lore.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This should NOT be confused with Dig bala of any graha in a horoscope. Dig bala is just the directional Strength of particular grahas, as below, at the time of birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That said when those grahas starts moving away from your lagna, the strength changes.</p><ul><li>Guru and Budha in lagna</li><li>Surya and Kuja in 10th</li><li>Shukra and Chandra in 4th</li><li>Shani in 7th</li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The above gets reduced as they move away from above position.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrocartography in vedic astrology are Directional lords and the cardinal directions which are called sapta or ashta matrikas - energy forms in 8 directions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=80ad96&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matrikas" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Matrikas - Wikipedia</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Understanding Matrikas - Dig Shakthis and their directions, and applying it to a horoscope is what can be considered as a real astrocartography in Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The benefits are immense.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">By changing the present lagna ( living place), in a particular direction, one can bring about change in the energy and the direction of that particular significance of a particular house, and reap the benefits.</p><pre class="prettyprint linenums">Om Brahmayai Namah
Om Maheswaryai Namah
Om Kaumaryai Namah
Om Vaisnavayai Namah
Om Varahayai Namah
Om Indranayai Namah
Om Chamundayai Namah
Om Chandikayai Namah
(The directions of matrikas are different in different vedic texts).

Om Asitanga Bhairavaya Namah
Om Ruru Bhairavaya Namah
Om Chanda Bhairavaya Namah
Om Krodha Bhairavaya Namah
Om Unmatta Bhairavaya Namah
Om Kapala Bhairavaya Namah
Om Bhisana Bhairavaya Namah
Om Samhara Bhairavaya Namah
</pre><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How to delineate from a particular horoscope, which significant house, whose benefits is to be reaped and accordingly, do that particular above <b>mantra prayog for that direction</b>, without changing the living place, is the work of an Astrologer, like me.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2018 07:25 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is a Pisces Sun, Sag Moon and Leo Ascendant like? Boy Aug 27 1983, Sion, 7.55am. Girl Jul 9 1982, Mumbai, 7.30am</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Is it possible to predict if two people will get married astrologically?</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Many questions, privately addressed to me fall in this category, as below</p><ol><li>We are in love with each other, but some problems, will we marry?</li><li>My parents had seen an alliance, will we marry?</li><li>Will my lost love come back and marriage happen?</li><li>I want her back, she should marry me only?</li><li>We love each other, our horoscope is not matching, create a fake horoscope, for a good match and marriage happen.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Let me clear this.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrology is a subject and it is NOT against Nature.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nature dictates that &#8220;One can love Many and marry Many&#8221;.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In vedic astrology 5th house rules love and 7th marriage, two different houses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The timing of events for two different houses need not start at the same time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For instance, the love-house time will start first and then 7th,in that case, it can be a love marriage, provided the yoga for love marriage is there in the chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If it starts, after, then, love will be after marriage, which can be called arranged marriage.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As there are many periods for marriage, the sequential choice of marriage, is based on time, at which point, there will be different suitors.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is NO One to One marriage choice, which can be asserted, only a prediction, can be made for compatibility and matching.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If you are destined, or it is the last marriage-period, for you to get married, the suitor in that period, will come and you can marry that person.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 10, 2018 08:28 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Can Vedic and Western astrology be correct in their outcomes and often give the same result?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is a good question.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is possible to read in both ways Vedic or Western, and be correct in the outcome and arrive at the same results.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How?</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The only difference between these two systems, at a chart level is the precession (ayanamsa).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then the usage of extra-Saturnian planets in western and the way the angles are handled in western, which somewhat is different from vedic in the interpretation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Give the above, using a placidus system on the tropical chart, as the starting point, one can read the present theme of the person, a particular significance of a life aspect.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then apply precession to the chart and read the house reading of that particular significance, from a vedic point of view, to know the inherent strength and weakness, the karmic quotient and inner strength of the person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Also delineate the time period from dasha system of vedic of when the actual event can happen.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Using present western astrology transits, one can find, whether the person would accept his/her karmic gift or overcome it, to go ahead to find his/her wish out of free will. This can be found using metonic-cycle of free will.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So both systems can find the correct outcome and give same results.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 11, 2018 12:28 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the rulership for Chakras? This has to be modified according to a person&#8217;s chart.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-0250d9c9d826181c44efdc2ebf459ae1" master_src="/img/qimg-0250d9c9d826181c44efdc2ebf459ae1" master_w="225" master_h="224" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mystic powers and Intuitive abilities are bestowed by the following yogas (planetary combinations).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The horoscope of any individual is mapped to the seven chakras of the person&#8217;s body. Depending on the different planet (graha) in that chakra, that person is bestowed with that mystic power. Is there any scientific cause?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Why bring the unscientific word called &#8216;scientific&#8217; into astrology. Lot had been told on that already.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Coming to your question.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Surya - Sun and Moon - Chandra, both have relationship at movement level. In a sidereal day, Chandra moves approximately 13.2 to 13.33 deg across the zodiac, against the rotation of Earth around Surya which is 360 deg.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Given above astronomical data, our Seers and Sages approximated it to 27 nakshatras (without adding Abhijit the 28th nakshatra), so each nakshatra is 13.333333 deg of an arc, in 360 deg.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then we have 9 grahas - namely Ketu, Shukra, Surya, Chandra, Kuja, Rahu, Guru, Shani and Budha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">No place for Pluto, Uranus or Neptune, as some newbie would have it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With these nine grahas, the zodiac sign was divided into 9 parts, which is 3.33333 of an arc and called pada.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This division by 9 is used for making the Navamsa D-9 chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Please search for Navamsa and its significance from one of my Q2A, to know more.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>This nakshatra division and its pada, is the corner stone of Vedic Astrology, which our poor cousin Western astrology do not have.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>With this nakshatra, scientific achievement, our Seers went ahead and equated space (13.33333 deg arc) to Time ( Dasha) system.</b></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 14, 2018 07:45 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">I have a Libra sun, Pisces moon, and a Libra Rising. Ayanamshas</b> as opposed to Lahiri Ayanamshas mostly used in Vedic System. The difference between two is about 6 minutes (Kala).</li><li>This system uses <b>Cusps</b> that is<b> house/ bhav beginnings</b> like Western Systems, as opposed to Vedic System which uses House Centres i.e. Bhav Madhyas.</li><li>This system uses <b>Placidus House system</b>.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>My observation are as below according to above points</b></p><ol><li>Parasara and KP gives same importance to Nakshatra divisions.</li><li>The division as per KP is peculiar. And the <b>total number arrived is WRONG, as per Placidus House system</b><a id="cite-WkrXL" href="#WkrXL" class="citation_link">[1]</a><b>, which has short and elongated houses</b>.</li><li>Spinning one&#8217;s own ayanamsa is a fashion of vedic researchers, so no comments on it.</li><li>Bhava chalit chart makes divisional charts impossible to make, so KP or Umang Taneja&#8217;s so called &#8220;Nadi Astrology&#8221; <b>should NOT use Varga</b> charts like Navamsa till Shodasamsa charts.</li><li>Placidus House system is western tropical. Bringing that into a &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221; and <b>equal nakshatra division</b>, begs explanation.</li><li>How is that a non-equal placidus house system, can be divided into equal nakshatra division, is my question?.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So, my take on <b>KP is, NO GOOD</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum:</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When the basics of KP is questionable at the very fundamentals as above, its borrowed axioms and postulations can be questioned. One may ask why 9 why not 7. The ancient Seers were smart enough that 11th from 9th, is 7th, meaning the fruits (11th) from Dharma (9th) is Spouse. I can bet 85% of the Indian astrologers would not know this.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Spouse is considered very important in the path of Dharma (Righteous path in life). Better half is always better.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The divisional chart is a kind of dissection on that particular aspect of life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are no house lordship or ownership and or aspects that can be read from a divisional chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Again 90% Indian astrologers read the divisional chart as a separate entity. Funny.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So one may ask what these represent. It represents the person&#8217;s state of mind, challenges and opportunities in that aspect of life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum:<br /></b>After the return from exile, Lord Rama had exiled Devi Sita to forest for some other reason. At that time, Lord Rama wanted to conduct a yagna, which was objected by Rishis, that he CANNOT do it, without his wife.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Yagna (<i>Ashwamedhayaga</i>) is considered to be very auspicious, which is the Dharma for a King, as it bestows prosperity to the Kingdom. For such an act also, the presence of wife is needed. Anyway Lord Rama did the yagna with a doll of Sita, which is another story.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">11th from 9th is 7th, is what it means, which was NOT explained to many, as divisional charts are intricate details, which the Rishis had ascribed to.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Other divisions also have same type of countings. Why or why not?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">KP system is an offshoot of Vedic astrology called Krishnamurthi Paddathi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Taking some information from sources, KP is as below</p><ol><li>KP system gives importance to the <b>Constellations</b> / <b>Stars</b> / <b>Nakshatras </b>divisions of the Zodiac which is obviously the most desired for precision.</li><li><b>Further it divides</b> each <b>Constellation</b> / <b>Star</b> / <b>Nakshatra</b> division into further 9 subdivisions called '<b>SUBS</b>'. These sub divisions are not equal divisions, but are as per the Vimshottari Dashas Divisions System.</li><li>K.P. System uses <b>K.P. Ayanamshas</b> as opposed to Lahiri Ayanamshas mostly used in Vedic System. The difference between two is about 6 minutes (Kala).</li><li>This system uses <b>Cusps</b> that is<b> house/ bhav beginnings</b> like Western Systems, as opposed to Vedic System which uses House Centres i.e. Bhav Madhyas.</li><li>This system uses <b>Placidus House system</b>.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>My observation are as below according to above points</b></p><ol><li>Parasara and KP gives same importance to Nakshatra divisions.</li><li>The division as per KP is peculiar. And the <b>total number arrived is WRONG, as per Placidus House system</b><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Steve-Hora">[1]</a></span><b>, which has short and elongated houses</b>.</li><li>Spinning one&#8217;s own ayanamsa is a fashion of vedic researchers, so no comments on it.</li><li>Bhava chalit chart makes divisional charts impossible to make, so KP or Umang Taneja&#8217;s so called &#8220;Astrology&#8221; <b>should NOT use Varga </b>charts like Navamsa till Shodasamsa charts.</li><li>Placidus House system is western tropical with unequal houses. Bringing that into a &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221;, <b>equal nakshatra and equal house division</b>, begs explanation.</li><li>How is that a non-equal placidus house system, can be divided into equal nakshatra division, is my question?.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So, my take on <b>KP is, NO GOOD</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum:</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When the basics of KP is questionable at the very fundamentals as above, its borrowed axioms and postulations can be questioned. KP astrology now takes another newer name as &#8220;Umang Taneja (ut) Astrology&#8221;. This is because the south Indian Nadi-Palm leaf are famous and by courtesy borrowed to promote KP and <b>ut&#8217;s astrology</b> in the name of Nadi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Disclaimer :</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>I DO NOT follow KP or ut&#8217;s so called &#8220;Astrology&#8221; in the name of Nadi.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Footnotes</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Steve-Hora">[1] </a></span><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=1be4c7&amp;url=http://www.astrologicalpredictions.ca/archive/house_size.htm" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="astrologicalpredictions.ca">Astrological Predictions Astrology House Size</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 28, 2018 05:33 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Which business would be best for me? /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Which Lord is more powerful between Lagna Lord, Rasi Lord and Nakshatra Lord in Vedic astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The question does not have any subjectivity or objectivity, let alone the context.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Assuming that the context of the question is to know, which lord would do good for a person.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna Lord is the recipient of anything.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rashi Lord is the thinker of actions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nakshatra Lord is the Dasha-Antara decider.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hope you understand.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is this typical analysis and mind-set in Indian astrologers, to decide and conclude something, and from there analyse the very details. This is counter productive or predictive. Or jump on to ad-literam lecturing or quoting from experience something which can be baseless.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">All are powerful in their own way and in a given situation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Take this scenario. Assuming Lagna lord is powerful, but time is bad. Then lagna lord will receive bad events only. This nulls his very powerfullness.<br />Or just if time is good, but rashi lord is weak, the thinking would not be enough, to accept change or change with free will. Then from Chandra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Whatever lagna, Pancha Mahapursh yoga comparatively is stronger than other yoga listed as Gaja Kesari, Hansa and Ruchak and what not.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Given that, the lordship of houses governed by yoga forming grahas, is more important than the very graha-by-name as Guru or Chandra, thinking or predicting Guru or Chandra as being great benefics. When an event does NOT happen in time for a person, he or she calls it bad time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When good events happen, time passes away fast.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So how we perceive in a given period, is what makes us think as good or bad about time. Perception can be due to the condition of the brain and mind, in a given situation, which is governed by Grahas. This is were Astrology can step in.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Grahas as such does NOT rule time. Grahas create a situation, where the mind is made to perceive as bad or good time, or fast or slow time movement.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So all the Dashas based on Moon is telling about perception of the mind in a given time, per see does not tell about the event.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Now the question can be easily answered. Change your perception and direction, then events will happen according to your liking, such that the so called bad can change to good.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To Change the perception and direction, is where a real, true and intuitive astrologer helps.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">All other astrologers would just simply analyse at length your horoscope, and then end up that your time is bad or good.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Feb 20, 2018 06:07 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What does the Kundali chart of the Sadhguru Shri Jaggi Vasudev convey? 3 September 1957 at 23:54, Mysore</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hi <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Akshara-S-2">Akshara S</a></span>,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Thanks for the A2A and also the privilege to analyse my Yogic Guru SadhGuru Jaggi VasuDev&#8217;s horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I had the great opportunity to be taught yoga and meditation in his esteemed yogic centre. Seeing from Earth, Surya will be in a section of the sky (namely star-nakshatra).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ancients vedic seers observed the pattern whenever a graha comes back to the same place, namely nakshatra. And saw something repeating, a guna of a person in a particular way.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Based on this geometrical pattern, seasons were also predicted.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This Geometrical pattern analysis was extended to human behavior and psychology, and from it Astrology came into being.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As any pattern repeats or continues from where it left, Seers found the connection between past birth or karma in these patterns and connected the karmic factor to birth. So Vedic seers used a fixed zodiac by minus-ing the present position to the original, using ayanamsa, so the karmic and fate factor is delineated.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That is why Vedic Astrology deals with fate and destiny, as it predicts from fixed zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Western astrology does not minus the ayanamsa, and just take the actual position of grahas as of now, so it is a moving zodiac, so it predicts the free-will cycle.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>May 27, 2018 Which one you are referring is of prime importance, at least for me, when synchronizing with transits.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To define the fundamentals. Transits are the incessant movement of grahas and its affectation on Rashi&#8217;s and on nakshtra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Dasha is a fixed time measurement from the birth chart based on nakshatra or other depending on the particular dasha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is nothing told in the vedic astrology books about the relationship. There is varshalphal which is based on sun&#8217;s yearly return (transit), which has some semblance of relationship with dasha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">My research into transits and Vimshottari dasha found a relationship, which I use in my accurate nadi-type predictions and which I call as Kalaa chakra or Nadi chakra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The above is what I call a relationship between transit and dasha.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jun 10, 2018 08:04 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What happens when Mars is in 12th house and Venus is in 6th house for Gemini ascendent?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Gemini ascendant, Mercury can be in any one of the 12 houses. It is true quora is free, so that I answer for free.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Many questioners think, just because Quora is free, questions should be answered for free.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Most of the free questioners do <b>not </b>upvote or follow, but ask free questions and expect the same. Many even do not get to know about the astrologer, but just ask. This can be seen from their new, incomplete or proxy or anonymous profiles.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But my free offering is for a public question on quora, not for private messages or email or any other communication channels. But then again people want free-private reading through email and they contact me on quora message.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I do free on email also, but for deserving cases, which I decide, so I accumulate good karma for me and my heirs.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Aug 23, 2018 01:34 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are some tips for do's and don'ts on Quora?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><ol><li>Never bother about the count of upvotes or followers</li><li>Check the profile of the questioner, before answering the question.</li><li>Choose the right question to answer, to showcase yourself.</li><li>Give importance to questions marked to you.</li><li>Be an expert of one field.</li><li>Do not try fancy Q&amp;A, by asking and answering only one question and fade away. And used to know about Spouse.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Preciseness is limited but sharp. Something like you are looking at a small area with a magnifying lens.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In that way Navamsa is precise for that significance.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For all novice and learners, Lagna is enough for preciseness.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum </b>: Navamsa applies for 30 deg equal house system, division from start of aswini nakshatra ONLY.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Signs are unequal, so divisional charts will not be applicable. Even lagna chart will be quixotic. Why? In unequal signs, some signs are elongated to 60 deg or above and some small nearly 22. Nakshatra and Dasha system will <b>not </b>fit in sign based system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Unequal sign topology was copied by modern vedic astrologers to mimic western astrologers.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Some calculate Lagna ONLY based on unequal sign which is western zodiac (Tropical). And all other Grahas including Sun position from start of Aries. But do reading with 30 deg house and nakshatra system. Funny, Quixotic and poorly knowledge.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Take Away</b>:</p><ol><li>In Vedic Astrology, everything will be measured from Start of Aries.</li><li>Start of Aries is calculated after taking ayanamsa into calculation.</li><li>All Grahas, including Sun and Lagna will be measured from start of Aries.</li><li>Parasara 30 deg equal house has properly defined house-life significance.</li><li>Equal house will help in delineating divisional charts properly.</li><li>All other systems are just fools talking stupid data. Period.</li></ol></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 25, 2018 08:22 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">When will I get a job? So we are all attached to this Earth and attracted by other Grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When attached to something or attracted, you have less Free Will.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If at all, if you have TOTAL Free will, you will fly-off this Earth. </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is no enemy or friend,nor permanent or temporary in Graha relationship. This applies for analysis of horoscopes.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Mundane matters, natural relationships (Friend and Enemy) to Grahas are applicable.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Assuming that we are analyzing a horoscope, a Graha (planet) can be an enemy of the said lagna lord and be in an enemy house. If it is in that enemy house, then it would be in an awkward position to show its effect, nor the house lord would allow it to work its effect.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In this situation, both the occupant and house lord would afflict the said horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ad-literam application of &#8220;Friend and Foe&#8221; axiom should not be applied.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 28, 2018 11:48 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the most accurate chart to use in astrology? For Sun it is <b>Suryay.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Note the names for 5th and 7th house Grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the your Love mantra will be</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Om Kleem </b>Suryay Shukray Namah<b>, </b>If Surya is your 5th lord and Shukra as your 7th lord.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is your best Vasikaran mantra, customized as per your horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When to utter or mantra prayog, matters a lot, for maximum and quick response. There are many, but Vimshottari Dasha system is the most popular one.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One can use any Dasha system, provided the basics of that should be understood and applied.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In Vimshottari, the Dasha lord is <b>not </b>directly connected to Graha lord.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Graha in a house, tells about its relative position and power, and in no way it tells about Kaala.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Dasha system tells about the Kaala as bad or good.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In essence, Grahas operate on a chart suo motu.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Kaala stands apart from Grahas and its power. And reading in that way, the remedies as mantras, will also be different.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vedic books consider Time as a separate entity and there upon came Kaaleswar as the lord of Kaala. Lord Bhairavaa is the archetypal Lord of Kaala.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>&#2349;&#2376;&#2352;&#2357; &#2327;&#2366;&#2351;&#2340;&#2381;&#2352;&#2368; &#2350;&#2306;&#2340;&#2381;&#2352;</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2384; &#2325;&#2366;&#2354;&#2366;&#2325;&#2366;&#2354;&#2366;&#2351; &#2357;&#2367;&#2343;&#2350;&#2361;&#2375;,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2325;&#2366;&#2354;&#2366;&#2309;&#2341;&#2368;&#2341;&#2366;&#2351;&#2366; &#2343;&#2368;&#2350;&#2361;&#2367;,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2340;&#2344;&#2381;&#2344;&#2379; &#2325;&#2366;&#2354; &#2349;&#2376;&#2352;&#2357;&#2366; &#2346;&#2381;&#2352;&#2330;&#2379;&#2342;&#2351;&#2366;&#2340;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Kaal Bhairava Gayatri Mantra:</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Om Kaalakaalaaya Vidmahe,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Kaalaatheethaaya dheemahi,</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tanno Kaala Bhairava Prachodayat</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From a horoscope, one can ascertain the bad and good time. And not in Jamini.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Mixing Jaimini with Vimshottari is again a modern fallacy.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hope it clear all novice and learners.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">And also some astrologers who use any system with mix and match (Parasara with Jaimini, with KP, with divisional charts, Natural karaka with Bhrigu Nadi), just to show the gullible that they know all.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 11, 2018 10:49 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What does Leo Sun, Cancer Moon, and Leo Rising mean?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The below reading is as per western astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Leo Rising and Leo Sun<br />Sun </b>as the planet ruler of Leo is in Leo itself. How this works on quora.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Let us assume, a marketing or HR guy, has a set of guys working for him.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">He keeps ready the question and answer.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One of the guy will post the question, and this person, who is the answer provider, logs in and pastes the answer.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then all other guys login and upvote, and <b><i>viola </i></b>the question and answer gets high views and upvotes.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So now the answerer becomes the most viewed guy and mvw on quora.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 16, 2018 06:47 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">If my date of birth is 30 Nov., am I a Sagittarius or an Ophiuchus? </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Do astrologers see/consider yogas and doshas of D1 chart only or of D2 and other divisional charts also?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For an erudite astrologer all charts matter, but &#8230;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">D1 - for all purposes is enough to delineate the yogas and doshas. That said in tamil, they say Rashi means also a heap of anything and everything. So the farmer now also will count his first heap as Rashi, in Tamil Nadu.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is true that Rashi is a heap of all the yogas and doshas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The divisional charts are too much math and microscopic, so for the novice astrologer, it will not be easy to comprehend the predictions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Due to the very microscopical nature, a different approach is there.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So it is a fight between ganith and phalith with any astrologer which distinguishes him from ordinary and destined ones.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It is now up to each astrologer to find how to read other divisional charts.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is no lordship, balas or drishti in divisional charts. So be it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I may not tell more about my research and my way, for reasons everybody know&#8230;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One has to put hard work for it, oneself, to know secrets.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 26, 2018 05:04 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the first prasna one should ask an astrologer to know whether that astrologer is a fake?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is a catch-22 situation for the seeker of astrology.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-123f0ebe65acc05a15f04b75026ecb8e" master_src="/img/qimg-123f0ebe65acc05a15f04b75026ecb8e" master_w="225" master_h="225" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I will answer for the benefit of the seeker, readers and people who get swindled in the name of astrology by fake ones.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The caveat : In answering this is, the astrologers reading this Q2A, will become smart, to give the seeker a good and consoling answer. So be pre-warned.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tell the astrologer that you have two questions, you have<b> problem in career</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If he/she replies with your own situation negatively, sugar-coated words, prescribe pujas, costly predictions and what not, then ask your health. Then you can decide then and there, that this is fake.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Then ask the next question about health, if above para repeats, then for sure he is a fake.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum: </b>If the astrologer is not interested to give your first free past-query, assume that he is more interested in consolidating the business transaction, than to prove.<br />Also if he/she takes time to predict or respond to the free question or prasna, assume that the astrologer is a novice or not interested in you by making you come after him/her, by playing a waiting game.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">More on this</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=0a9a07&amp;url=https://www.astrologyoftheancients.com/real-astrologers/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="astrologyoftheancients.com">How to Tell Real Astrologers From Fakes - Astrology of</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 26, 2018 06:49 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Why did my Quora notifications get deleted?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I had seen this happening on Quora.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-73fd41d8015b47a9a4acca849dc721b9" master_src="/img/qimg-73fd41d8015b47a9a4acca849dc721b9" master_w="168" master_h="300" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>One Case</b> : There was a notification from quora, that a person had commented on my answer. And all the doshas like Bhakoot and Nadi etc are based on Chandra only, ignoring all other Graha&#8217;s matching.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">What if Chandra in the individual chart signifies some other thing? is a open question for astrologers&#8230;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Pitfalls in horoscope matching</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Matching both horoscope is nice to hear and do. But there are 12 houses, 12 lagnas and 9 grahas. And multiplying this by two, for both charts and finding each and every compatibility for each chart, is a herculean task.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are clients who ask ALL but ALL, especially from the girl&#8217;s chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Destiny</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">End of the day (marriage), one marries with some matching with guna milan count or porutha with some dosha and end up living together.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So what is the hue and cry.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are flaws in the above procedure.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>What is the middle path</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nakshatra lord and House lord can be matched.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The <b>1st and 7th</b> lord in one horoscope can be matched to <b>7th and 1st in the other.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">5th can be checked in both for children.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">12th also to be checked in these modern days for bed pleasures.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This should be enough.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Other incompatibility can be sorted by destiny or by the two, using their brains.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Not matched, but still love each other, understand the mismatch and solve it or put up with it or go your own way.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. <i>&#2340;&#2341;&#2366;&#2360;&#2381;&#2340;&#2369;</i>.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Oct 26, 2018 period, makes it sensitive to accurate time of birth and ayanamsa.</li><li>Presumptive ayus of different nakshatra configuration</li><li>Arbitrary nakshatra grouping</li><li>Confusion on Repeat of cycle.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>So KCD is not good. The nakshatras of Ketu are Ashwini, Magha and Moola.The South node of the Rahu-Ketu axis is called as Ketu</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu denotes one's ego and the placement in the horoscope, indicates to the person, in which field of life, should work towards,to Moksha or liberation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu will give sudden and unexpected changes in life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu is an enemy of Chandra, Surya and Kuja.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Is a friend of Shani, Shukra and Budha. Ketu is neutral to Guru.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu is a spiritual Graha. Good influence of Ketu will give spiritual achievements, healing, spiritual and tantric power.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu Maha dasha is seven years. His Gemstone is Cat`s eye.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ketu, if placed favorably in horoscope, brings a lot of luxury, wisdom and intuition to a person. If unfavorable, he causes depression, poor concentration, boundless worries, anxiety and ghost related problems.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-69df812a2807986975611ef14e02bcd4" master_src="/img/qimg-69df812a2807986975611ef14e02bcd4" master_w="300" master_h="168" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 07, 2018 09:18 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the effects of Ketu in the sixth house? Papakartari Yoga in Vedic astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For simplicity sake, I will generalize it as Kartari Yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Kartari means to remove, shear or to cut.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The yoga is formed by hemming of a Graha on both sides namely 2nd and 12th, with Grahas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If the 2nd and 12th house from the said Graha, has good Grahas, for the lagna, it is called Shubh-Kartari Yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If the 2nd and 12th house from the said Graha, has bad Grahas, for the lagna, it is called Papa-Kartari Yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If the 2nd and 12th house from the said Graha, has good and bad Grahas, for the lagna, it is called &#2350;&#2367;&#2358;&#2381;&#2352;&#2367;&#2340;-Kartari Yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For example : If a good Graha like Waxing Chandra has in its 2nd house, Shukra and has in 12th, Budha, assuming all these grahas are good for this lagna lord, then a Shubh-Kartari Yoga is formed.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img If bad, it will imprison the person, for no fault of his/her or make wander headless in search of moksha, without purpose.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So be it. <i>Tathastu</i>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b><i>Reference : Ketu and Moksha</i></b><a id="cite-vguME" href="#vguME" class="citation_link">[1]</a></p><p class="qtext_citation_lead">Footnotes</p><p class="citation" id="vguME"><a href="#cite-vguME" class="citation_index">[1] </a><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=45614e&amp;url=http://vedicartandscience.com/ketuinvedicastrology/?fb_action_ids%3D2113614988891447%26fb_action_types%3Dog.comments%26fbclid%3DIwAR3WAZEt8ph_UAYAtOG4iROHRkmQtg8st5Mys8VY1uRrMWfeZ64LdosOaTk" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="vedicartandscience.com">Rahu / Ketu and the Sun</a></span></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Nov 18, 2018 01:35 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">In Vedic astrology, can anyone explain in detail each house? Sanchita (accumulated), Prarabdha (fructifying) and Kriyamana or Agami (current).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Karma is action using one&#8217;s energy with an intention. The intention could be bad or good. And that intention is stored in each individual&#8217;s sub-conscious mind and serves as the karmic memory.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">With this karmic memory, one is born. That birth with its Vedic astrology horoscope, is embedded with its karma, which is sanchita and has its effect as good or bad as perceived by the individual.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Karma is connected with time. Time as noted as Dasha and Antara, and in that prescribed time, karma takes its toll.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrological remedies are not a breach of the above explained karma.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As an astute astrologer, if one can read the karma and its time of action, it is also possible and easy to read remedies from the chart itself.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Remedies prescribed by an astrologer should be a combination of spiritual, psychological, mental and physical to remedy the intention of that karma. Then the sanchita karma <b>energy </b>can be <b>nullified</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This does <b>NOT </b>nullify the <b>bad time </b>of that bad (sanchita) karma. Why, the explanation is simple. The intention was done in a previous time and time cannot be substituted by a remedial action.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Without understanding this astrologers give remedies and seekers think that by spending some energy (money or dhana), one can negate bad karma and enjoy all the fruits of good karma. So be it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But there is a way to change bad time also to good time. And that is the real astrological remedy for the bad karma.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Theedhum nandrum pirar thara vaara</b></p><ul><li>Tamil: &#2980;&#3008;&#2980;&#3009;&#2990;&#3021; &#2984;&#2985;&#3021;&#2993;&#3009;&#2990;&#3021; &#2986;&#3007;&#2993;&#2992;&#3021; &#2980;&#2992; &#2997;&#3006;&#2992;&#3006;.</li><li>Literal: Good or bad, it doesn't come from others.</li><li>Meaning: What happens to one, good or bad, it doesn't come from the actions of others, but from their own deeds.</li></ul><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-3c504205437bf4d3c60eade4ef378d32" master_src="/img/qimg-3c504205437bf4d3c60eade4ef378d32" master_w="201" master_h="251" /></div></div></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Dec 25, 2018 06:50 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What are the best astrological remedies?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The prediction and the remedy is there in your chart itself.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So something best for you should be unique to your chart ONLY.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Remedy is due to Graha Charam (Planetary movement) - Transits.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Another one is by time which is the current Dasha and Antara.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How the current Dasha affects the 12 houses should be understood from the horoscope itself.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How it is felt by the person can be gauged by lagna, Chandra and Surya positions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So this dosha and its remedies is not connected with free will.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nor some general lal-kitabic remedy will work out.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The remedy should be spiritual, psychological, mental and Physical. Dasha in astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtottari Dasha has a basic flaw, which I will come to that later.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtottari total dasha years is 108 lunar days.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vimshottari is Udu dasha based on nakshatra and total dasha years is 120 solar days.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But you find people living for 108 lunar years or more or near 120 solar years. So it looks like Vimshottari is correct to use, in Kali Yuga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtottari is based on lunar tithi, which allocates different years to different grahas, excluding Ketu. Including Rahu and excluding Ketu, does not make any logical sense. The reason could be Ketu eclipses Chandra and Ashtottari is based on Chandra&#8217;s tithi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But as such the phase or tithi for Chandra or any other graha is there, except for Surya. Because Surya can be only at zero phase from itself. This could be the reason for Surya being given 6 and Chandra given 12+3 = 15 lunar years in Ashtottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To use Ashtottari effectively, this above anomaly has to be corrected, making equal to Vimshottari&#8217;s 120 years, which is naturally correct for Kali Yuga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This can be corrected as below.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rahu is allocated 17. Ketu none. Rahu and Ketu as a unit will be allocated 24 as per tithi calculations. So 24 minus 17 is 7.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So 7 lunar years can be allocated to Ketu.<br />Surya can be 6 lunar years, as Chandra has 15.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The total should come to 120 lunar years, so remaining 5 years can be given to Lagna. Why lagna?. Lagna is a position from Surya in a chart. As Surya has less years, its mathematical counterpart Lagna, which has phases with Surya can be given the remaining years.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So now the new Ashtottari can be Sn - 6 lunar years, L - 5, Mn - 15, Mrs - 8, R - 17, J - 10, St - 19, Mer - 12, K - 7, V - 21. Making the total as 120 lunar years.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Hope Shukra Acharya would not mind this change to make better prediction with his algorithm than Vimshottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum: </b>Lagna will be the first Dasha balance of years, followed by Surya and Chandra, and others.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jan 09, 2019 09:37 PM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Does That is from Full Moon to New Moon (Dark).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Shukla Paksha is Waxing Moon, when Chandra increases in size. That is from New Moon to Full Moon.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Muhurtha selection, this Paksha and Tithi matters.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Everybody will be born in any one of the Paksha and Tithi (Moon Phase). This will NOT per see decide any difference.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each Paksha or Tithi is endowed with its own &#8220;Chandra Kala&#8221; Energy, which is pure and sublime.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But you will find astrologers, assume something from Muhurtha and apply to fixed karmic chart which is a horoscope.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There goes down another fallacy and blunder of Vedic Astrologers.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So what is the difference. The different energy that is assigned for that Thithi. So be it. Tathastu.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Feb 08, 2019 07:04 AM PST</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Is applying Ashtottari dasha to relevant charts really meaningful? Does it give an accurate interpretation?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtottari Dasha is of two types, one based on nakshatra (conditional) and the Tithi-Pravesha Ashtottari Dasha based on tithi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The first one based on nakshatra, is used as a contemporary to Vimshottari dasha, with some conditions in the chart. The sequence of dasha is different from Vimshotari, which starts from Aridhara nakshatra.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But applying the same nakshatra-dasha sequence to Tithi Pravesha by PVR Narasimha Rao in <b>Jagannatha Hora </b>software is <b>questionable and WRONG</b>, as this is based on Tithi, and its lords follow a different sequence.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is a great anomaly. This has to be corrected at Tithi Ashtottari dasha system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Ashtottari Dasha (ruled by Shukra) had been a <b>closely guarded secret Dasha, </b>because it applies for present worldly (money and sensuous) matters than to attain moksha, which is the prime aim of Vimshottari system (ruled by Guru for moksha).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So Ashtottari Dasha is highly relevant and accurate than Vimshottari in present world, where Shukra rules, when people are going after too much money, wealth and sensuous pleasures.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I use Ashtottari also with greater accuracy than Vimshottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>So be it. Tathastu.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum</b> :</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Who is the guru of Ashtottari ?</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Take the Sun's period + the moon's period in Ashtottari, that is, Sun (6) + Moon (15) = 21. Which graha has 21 dasa years? Venus. So, Venus is the guru for Ashtottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">And for Vimshottari ? Sun ( 6) + moon ( 10) = 16 in Vimshottari. Which graha has 16 dasa years in the Vimshottari scheme? It is Jupiter. So Guru is the guru of Vimshottari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So in Kaliyuga, most people, go after money, power, position, sensuous pleasures, their horoscopes should be predicted with Ashtottari Dasha. Thethi in tamil is used colloquially.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This tithi is 30 in numbers, and it is measured in 12 degrees and its multiples, from Sun to Moon. So total is 30 * 12 = 360, completes a full cycle of tithis.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The waxing (growing) phase of Chandra is called Shukla Paksha and the waning (decreasing) phase is Krishna paksha.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Tithi decided by Surya-Chandra (Father-Mother) of these earthlings, their attitude, behavior and the time cycle.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nowadays only death-tithi date is followed by many. Other activities and its connectivity to horoscope is not given importance or not known. May be due to lost traditions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">A person born in some tithis are riktha, namely 4th, 9th and 14th. Especially the krishna paksha of above tithis, are not auspicious.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In muhurtha, also these tithis are avoided for auspicious works.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are remedies for person born in above tithis especially the above ones, using special Mantra-Yantra-Tantra based on Surya-Chandra time cycle.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Extrapolating on above lines will surely lead to the connectivity of the micro-cosmos (person) with macro-cosmos (god). <b>So be it. Trimsamsa chart?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Trimsamsa chart or D-30 is to know the evils one will face in boothas and in turn grahas, except Surya, Chandra, Rahu and Ketu. Tathastu.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Going further using the Varmam points as prescribed by Sage Agasthiya, one can cure the above diseases. Akasha is neutral. Prithivi joins Jala.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">These Pancha Boothas are in turn mapped to Kuja, Budha, Guru, Shani and Shukra. Surya and Chandra are luminaries, so not part of the boothas.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But Surya and Chandra, will play a role in timing (Kaala) of the disease and as well through genetics, as Surya is Father and Chandra is Mother.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Rahu and Ketu do not belong to pancha boothas and opposite of luminaries, so they cause mysterious or emergency or unknown diseases. Rahu Ketu in a way blocks as per karmic-ness the very Kaala to get cured.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This way the atma goes through the whole process of health and disease.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">These Pancha boothas are mapped to the fingers of a person. Thumb being Fire, etc etc. Check my other answer for mapping. Only 10 fingers, as Rahu and Ketu are not given one each.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The left part of the human body is Shakthi, Female and right side is Male. ArthaNari-Eeshwarar Roopa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From Trimsamsa, the mapping of disease is done to body parts and Ayurvedic treatment of balancing of doshas can be done.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Using Naadi or Varmam, one can give pressure to the points as per Trimsamsa to cure disease.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">On top of all, the time to cure is decided by the karma of that person. Till then he/she suffers and dies. If it is good karma, that person meets the right medical practitioner, to get cured.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The time for cure, is decided by Surya-Chandra with Tithi-timing at Tithi-based dasha level. On a daily basis Pancha Pakshi decides, which can be based on Tithi, not on nakshatra and Vara.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Mar 17, 2019 06:44 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Do Hindus worship women?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The very divinity of Hinduism is Adi-Shakthi, the Maha Tripura Sundari.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The trinities namely Lord Shiva, Lord Vishnu and Lord Brahma meditate upon her.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">She is formless and the epitome of Adhi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">She is represented as Shree Chakra, and resides at the center of it, the Bindu.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-57b14f1aa7a5a29003878491d3b9a826" master_src="/img/qimg-57b14f1aa7a5a29003878491d3b9a826" master_w="480" master_h="480" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Kleem in her mantra represents Maha Kali.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Shreem represents Maha Lakshmi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Hreem represents Saraswati.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The downward triangles in above Shree Chakra are five, representing feminine power.
