Is there any similarity to decans of Western astrology?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=fbba3e&amp;url=https://youtu.be/L5NCD05E2dE" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link">https://youtu.be/L5NCD05E2dE</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Decans in Western astrology is dividing the sign into 3 (equal?) parts of 10 degree each.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Read more about Decans at <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=3c0b93&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decan_(astrology)" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Decan (astrology) - Wikipedia</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Drekkana in Vedic Astrology is also dividing equal houses into 3 equal parts. Each part is called a drekkana.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Read more about Drekkana at <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=c0e1e2&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Drekkana" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Drekkana - Wikipedia</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The similarity ends there.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The allocation of lords to decans and drekkana are different for each system.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Different Decans tell about a person or country whether he/she is evil minded, sinner and wrathful. If trend is mixed then native will be lazy, back biter and ill-behaved. But if all three (among Sun, Moon and Ascendant) rises in benefic Decante (and their lord of Decante are also powerful) then native would be blessed, intelligent, soft spoken and successful.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The division and allocation of Jagannatha Drekkana is very similar to western astrology&#8217;s decans.</p><blockquote><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-8383d5ee8620d159dd21609f42de3f6c" master_src="/img/qimg-8383d5ee8620d159dd21609f42de3f6c" master_w="390" master_h="49" /></div></div><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-fd2349cb41e37819ab6047979129af14" master_src="/img/qimg-fd2349cb41e37819ab6047979129af14" master_w="373" master_h="53" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The above slokas from Brihat Parasara Hora Shastra points to a Jagannatha Drekkana.</p></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The drekkana of vedic astrology are assigned to Naarda, Agastya and Dhurvasa. Narada as Devarsi, Agastya as Brahmarsi and Durvasa as Mahrsi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each Rishi has an inert talent and guna to create the world again from the end of mahapralaya ( or destruction).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Decans are mapped to Countries in Western astrology. When drekkana is mapped to each country, one can know the intricate quality of each country and its behavior.<b> So be it.</b></p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 23, 2019 11:40 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How can I make karma my friend?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">You can. First you need to understand it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Now as a man is like this or like that,<br />according as he acts and according as he behaves, so will he be;<br />a man of good acts will become good, a man of bad acts, bad;<br />he becomes pure by pure deeds, bad by bad deeds;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">And here they say that a person consists of desires,<br />and as is his desire, so is his will;<br />and as is his will, so is his deed;<br />and whatever deed he does, that he will reap.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#8212; <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=14520f&amp;url=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brihadaranyaka_Upanishad" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="wikipedia.org">Brihadaranyaka Upanishad</a></span>, 7th Century BCE</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The karmas are of three type, namely, the past - Sanchitta, present - Parabda, and future - Agami</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>1. Sanchitta</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is accumulated past actions or karmas to come to pass in this birth (manifestation) or in future births.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sanchitta is the storehouse of every action you have ever done, in all the lifetimes you have ever lived. These are all of the unresolved past actions waiting to reach resolution.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>2. Parabda</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This is the present action: what you are doing now, in this lifetime and its result.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>3. Agami</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Future karma result from your present actions are called agami karma. As you attempt to resolve past karma, you unavoidably create new karmas that you may or may not be able to resolve in your present life. If you don't resolve them now, they will go into the storehouse to be resolved in a future life.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">To make karma your friend</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Best way : Attain nirvana like Lord Buddha. No response, no new karma, emptied all old karma, and do not even do good or bad karma in present birth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Better way : Push sanchitta to future by agamic ways. Enjoy good karma and spend energy (e.g. money) for your present bad karma. E.g. Smoking and suffer.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Worst way: Just don&#8217;t care about all of above, live life as it comes, enjoy and suffer.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Each one to his/her own way. So be it.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">End of the day the question that will be asked is : Q: Why all these karmas ? - A: Will stay forever as long as action is.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Apr 25, 2019 08:40 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What roles Kundali?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Death can be Akaal or Kaal maran.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Akaal means untoward death by accidents, self-infliction, natural disasters, etc.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Kaal maran means, the death happened by time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Both Kaal and Akaal maran is there in every chart, when that dasha-antara operates in SamayaAmsa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That said, Kaal, means the duration, which can be extended using pranic techniques like yoga and meditation.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Astrology is a science to help overcome Akaal maran, extend Kaal, to do good karmic activities and continue in coming lives.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As an Astrologer, I consider inauspicious to tell about a person&#8217;s longevity, given the possibility of extending life by yoga.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Nevertheless, it is possible to tell from a chart, the Akaal and Kaal maran Kaalas (duration) from Lagna, Navamsa and Ashtamsa and SamayaAmsa.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From that one can ascertain, that person&#8217;s longevity status.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I had recently a case, who was on death bed, with Akaal maran time running. Which is the one to know about wealth from a Vedic horoscope, Indu or Shri (Lakshmi) Lagna?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Lagna is a mathematical co-ordinate in degree and min in the zodiac.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are many lagnas. Lagna means starting point.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">In a Lagna or Rashi chart, the 1st house is delineated by the lagna point.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Some special lagnas are calculated based on Lagna chart (D1).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Two among them is Indu lagna and Shri lagna for wealth.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Indu lagna</b></p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Kalidas in Uttara Kalarita (Ch. IV. 27) has briefly described the method of calculation of Indu Lagna and its result as follows:</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">&#2309;&#2352;&#2381;&#2325;&#2366;&#2344;&#2381;&#2344;&#2366;&#2327;&#2330;&#2335;&#2360;&#2381;&#2340;&#2344;&#2369;&#2352;&#2381;&#2332;&#2344;&#2344;&#2335;&#2307; &#2326;&#2375;&#2335;&#2366;&#2351;&#2344;&#2306; &#2360;&#2381;&#2351;&#2369;&#2360;&#2381;&#2340;&#2344;&#2379;-<br />&#2358;&#2381;&#2330;&#2344;&#2381;&#2342;&#2381;&#2352;&#2366;&#2342;&#2381;&#2349;&#2366;&#2327;&#2381;&#2351;&#2346;&#2351;&#2379;&#2307; &#2325;&#2381;&#2354;&#2376;&#2325;&#2381;&#2351;&#2350;&#2367;&#2344;&#2361;&#2371;&#2330;&#2381;&#2331;&#2367;&#2359;&#2381;&#2335;&#2306; &#2357;&#2367;&#2342;&#2381;&#2351;&#2379;&#2352;&#2381;&#2351;&#2342;&#2381;&#2327;&#2371;&#2361;&#2350;&#2381;&#2404;<br />&#2340;&#2342;&#2381;&#2352;&#2366;&#2358;&#2380; &#2340;&#2369; &#2357;&#2367;&#2346;&#2366;&#2346;&#2358;&#2379;&#2349;&#2344;&#2326;&#2327;&#2375; &#2325;&#2379;&#2335;&#2368;&#2358;&#2381;&#2357;&#2352;&#2306; &#2340;&#2344;&#2381;&#2357;&#2340;&#2375;,<br />&#2330;&#2375;&#2340;&#2381;&#2346;&#2366;&#2346;&#2375; &#2340;&#2369; &#2360;&#2361;&#2360;&#2381;&#2340;&#2381;&#2352;&#2358;&#2307; &#2326;&#2354;&#2326;&#2327;&#2375; &#2340;&#2369;&#2306;&#2327;&#2375;&#2365;&#2346;&#2367; &#2325;&#2379;&#2335;&#2368;&#2358;&#2381;&#2357;&#2352;&#2350;&#2381;&#2404;&#2404;</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-7855f3b9f3b048a7f3d83eeda67012a6" master_src="/img/qimg-7855f3b9f3b048a7f3d83eeda67012a6" master_w="698" master_h="100" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><i>**The planets Rahu and Ketu are not used in this calculation.</i></p><ul><li>After this, find out the zodiac sign (rashi) falling in the ninth house of the Lagna Chart; and write down the value of the lord of ninth house.</li><li>Find out the zodiac sign (rashi) falling in the ninth house of the Moon Chart; and write down the value of ninth house lord in Moon Chart.</li><li>Add both these values; and then, divide it by 12 and note down the remainder, which will be between 0 to 11.</li><li>Count the number from the position of the Moon; and the house identified will be the Indu Lagna or Dhana Lagna or Wealth Ascendant.</li></ul></blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Fallacy of Indu lagna</b></p><ul><li>The allotment of Kaalas is arbitrary.</li><li>The total Kaalas is 83, which is <b>NOT fully </b>divisible by 12.</li><li>It <b>SHOULD</b> be 84, which is fully divisible by 12. This will make the reminder 0 or 12, which is logical in cyclic mathematical calculations.</li><li>If it is 84, then 1 more Kaalas has to be allotted to some graha. Which one?</li><li><b>There is NO Dasha specially for Indu Lagna, to delineate time of happening.</b></li></ul><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Sri (Lakshmi) Lagna</b></p><ol><li>Lakshmis are eight in number : Ashta Lakshmi.</li><li>There are eight prosperity or wealth in life.</li><li>Sri lagna is calculated mathematically properly in deg min.</li><li>Parashara, the Maharishi of Astrology, in the <b>BPHS </b>discusses the Sri Lagna.</li><li><b>Sri Lagna has a special Dasha, namely Sudasa</b> or for delineating the time of fructify of different wealth or prosperity.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For Wealth prediction using Sudasa and Sri lagna, contact me.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Sri lagna is the right one, to judge Wealth in a horoscope.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>May 17, 2019 07:50 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How long have you been a part of QPP?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">I am not part of the QPP program of Quora.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">QPP is as below</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The Quora Partner Program is an invite only program that rewards members of the program for asking engaging, thoughtful questions. This is 24 horas or hours.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The zeroth point for a day is the sunrise time.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As per panchang or Hindu calendar, each start of a hora on a day, is allocated as per the week day. The next hora after sunrise is based on the below sequence.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Surya, Shukra, Chandra, Shani, Guru and Kuja for Sunday.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The proof for this sequence of week day allocation to different grahas is logical and one can find that in this Q2A.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/How-were-weekdays-named-in-such-a-sequence">How were weekdays named in such a sequence?</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">BUT, the question is&#8230;</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When and How the first Sunday started.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Why today, which is a Wednesday, not be Sunday or Tuesday?.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There is NO logical or mathematical answer to above two questions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>The sequence of week days is right logically, but start of week names is NOT logical.</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So if some one says, now is Saturday - Shani Hora, do not cut your hair or do this or that, then this is fallacy.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Anything based on week day or vaar is totally wrong as per me, and stand to be right.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">How to resolve this?.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">One has to define what a hour will do, observe its significance and then one can calibrate that as Tuesday or Saturday. But nobody would follow it, as accepted week days are too common to be changed.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But there is another way.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Take the graha rise at horizon each day, and one can assign the first hora to that graha and follow above sequence. In this scenario my <b>Kaal Hora or Kaala Hora</b> is the best.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jun 18, 2019 09:29 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Which divisional chart is the most important chart in astrology? But we consider in Vedic Astrology, Full Moon or Pournami as the best tithi day.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">If we apply the same logic then Combust of any Graha should be the best. are astrological houses?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Vedic Astrological houses are 12 in numbers.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Western astrology will add another 13th one as per scientific NASA data.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The 12 houses in Vedic starts from Mesha (Aries) till Meena (Pisces).</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">There are different type of house systems in Vedic and Western.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Equal houses with &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221;, taking into account the Lahiri ayanamsa, is the widely followed one.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">But that very division of houses or signs as 30 degrees in equal houses and unequal houses as in other house systems are just imaginary divisions.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As such the graha ruling a particular house (equal or unequal) knows when to influence the person&#8217;s horoscope, mathematically.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So the degree of the graha is more important than even the house.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">That way, in suo-moto the graha will influence the person in it&#8217;s time.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jun 21, 2019 06:20 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">Is an From 20 39 it is middle age of non acceptance and denial. From 40 to 59 it is acceptance. From 60 it is back to childish ways.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jun 27, 2019 09:15 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">What is the basis of horoscopes?</span></div><div><strong>Content: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext"><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The question is about the basis, NOT what it is.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">It has two parts Horo - Hora - Hour. This facilitated to understand each human as per birth, to predict.</li><li>Vedic Astrology extended these to Past, Present and Future births, based on Karma. u-text-align--start">KP astrology is a subset of Vedic Astrology.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The difference is KP uses a way of dividing Dasha into sub-values and uses sub-lord to decide.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">My take on KP is as below</p><blockquote><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">KP system is an offshoot of Vedic astrology called Krishnamurthi Paddathi.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Taking some information from sources, KP is as below</p><ol><li>KP system gives importance to the <b>Constellations</b> / <b>Stars</b> / <b>Nakshatras </b>divisions of the Zodiac which is obviously the most desired for precision.</li><li><b>Further it divides</b> each <b>Constellation</b> / <b>Star</b> / <b>Nakshatra</b> division into further 9 subdivisions called '<b>SUBS</b>'. These sub divisions are not equal divisions, but are as per the Vimshottari Dashas Divisions System.</li><li>K.P. System uses <b>K.P. Ayanamshas</b> as opposed to Lahiri Ayanamshas mostly used in Vedic System. The difference between two is about 6 minutes (Kaala).</li><li>This system uses <b>Cusps</b> that is<b> house/ bhav beginnings</b> like Western Systems, as opposed to Vedic System which uses House Centres i.e. Bhav Madhyas.</li><li>This system uses <b>Placidus House system which is western tropical</b>. Krishnamurthy was fascinated by western astrology,so he used tropical house system. Parasara does NOT advocate that.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>My observation are as below according to above points</b></p><ol><li>Parasara and KP gives same importance to Nakshatra divisions.</li><li>The division as per KP is peculiar. And the <b>total number arrived is WRONG, as per Placidus House system</b><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/profile/Steve-Hora">[1]</a></span><b>, which has short and elongated houses</b>.</li><li><b><i>The number used in KP, 249 is WRONG. 9 nakshatra of 9 division will give 81. Multiple by 3 gives 243, for whole zodiac. It should be 243. 249 is wrongly arrived using western house system, which is absurd.</i></b></li><li>Spinning one&#8217;s own ayanamsa is a fashion of vedic researchers, so no comments on it.</li><li>Bhava chalit chart makes divisional charts impossible to make, so KP or Umang Taneja&#8217;s so called &#8220;Astrology&#8221; <b>should NOT use Varga </b>charts like Navamsa till Shodasamsa charts.</li><li>Placidus House system is western tropical with unequal houses. Bringing that into a &#8220;Start of Aries&#8221;, <b>equal nakshatra and equal house division</b>, begs explanation.</li><li>How is that a non-equal placidus house system, can be divided into equal nakshatra division, is my question?.</li></ol><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">So, my take on <b>KP is, NO GOOD</b>.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Addendum:</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">When the basics of KP is questionable at the very fundamentals as above, its borrowed axioms and postulations can be questioned. In addition, two &#8220;chaayaa grahas&#8221; (shadow grahas) namely Rahu and Ketu is included. These are North and South node of the Axis.<br />Rahu and Ketu are just mathematical points, where the path of Sun and Moon crosses.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Grahas in Vedic Astrology are given ownership of different houses from Aries till Pisces.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Refer this <span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=e1d8bc&amp;url=https://stevehora.com/vedic/what-is-a-graha/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="stevehora.com">Steve Hora Astrologer | What is a Graha?</a></span></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><span class="qlink_container"><a href="https://www.quora.com/_/redirect?sig=7e8da3&amp;url=https://stevehora.com/category/vedic/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank" onclick="return Q.openUrl(this);" class="external_link" data-qt-tooltip="stevehora.com">To learn more about astrology, refer this url</a></span>.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Jul 26, 2019 09:49 PM PDT</span></div></p><hr /><p><h2>Answer</h2><div><strong>Question: </strong><span class="rendered_qtext">How will be my married life when retrograde Saturn is in 5th, Venus in 9th, Mars and Jupiter in the 12th house of a Libra ascendant? Ananta means joy.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">USA rises and shines and been a great country and will be forever.<br />God <b>blesses </b>America.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">Below is &#8220;Republic of India&#8221; chart.</p><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="portrait qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-c2c6232a9655c3d613f6171c364bfc4b" master_src="/img/qimg-c2c6232a9655c3d613f6171c364bfc4b" master_w="794" master_h="1123" /></div></div><div class="ui_qtext_image_outer"><div class="qtext_image_wrapper"><img class="landscape qtext_image zoomable_in_feed" src="/img/qimg-69f77dec30c6ee96d176f233965eb53e" master_src="/img/qimg-69f77dec30c6ee96d176f233965eb53e" master_w="434" master_h="205" /></div></div><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The lagna lord is Guru for India, and is in 11th, Being 10th also Guru gives benefits to itself and its people.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start"><b>Relationship of USA and India</b></p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">USA lagna lord is Budha and India&#8217;s it is Guru. Budha is in 10th house of Guru. India is loved by USA and vice-versa. This is due to retrogression of Budha in India&#8217;s chart.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">This very retrograde of Budha had helped India, to accept USA as a father figure. If not, astrologically it cannot be, as Budha and Guru story goes.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The very exchange of Budha and Guru in USA chart, is the foundation of a great relationship between these two countries.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">The 7th lord Budha for USA and Guru for India, is good for relationship.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">As per Samaya Amsa for India, from July 2011 it was good time for Guru. So the relationships became stronger with USA.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">From June 2019, it became stronger, when Guru became powerful in its 10th house, and great things will happen.</p><p class="qtext_para u-ltr u-text-align--start">For USA, as per Samaya Amsa, the timing is, from Apr 2017 till Dec 2019, good for power and progress. From Jan 2020 till May 2022 great benefits accrue. From June 2022 till Mar 2023, USA will protect its people from foreign enemies.</p></span></div><div><strong>Creation time: </strong><span>Sep 24, 2019 05:34 AM PDT</span></div></p><hr /></div>
